Sr. B2B Content Specialist

2Base Technologies Pvt Ltd
Infopark

A senior B2B content specialist role at 2Base Technologies, responsible for enforcing the company's written voice across technical and business audiences, ensuring technical credibility and commercial relevance through long-form content and leadership-voice writing.

3-5 YearsB2B ContentSEOAI Tools
Apply by: 10 Apr 2026

Sr. B2B Content Specialist

2Base Technologies is at a deliberate stage of building its marketing function, and this role owns the written voice of that function end to end. We are a technology services company with over 15 years of delivery experience, working with mid-market and enterprise clients across the United States and the United Kingdom. Our work spans AI implementation, custom software development, legacy system modernisation, and operational transformation.

What This Role Exists to Do

This role does not invent the voice. It operationalises, applies, and enforces it across all written output: long-form content that earns search traffic, content written in the voice of senior leadership for professional publishing, and the quality standard for everything written that leaves this company.

Audience: Technical leaders and business decision-makers at mid-market companies (CTOs, IT Directors, Founders, COOs, Operations leaders) who evaluate architecture decisions or are accountable for technology outcomes.

What You Will Own

  • All long-form written content: pillar pages, blogs, playbooks, decision frameworks, and use-case libraries targeting senior decision-makers in the US and UK.
  • Written content produced in the voice of senior leadership for professional platforms.
  • The 2Base content voice, including auditing all published content to ensure brand standards.
  • Content briefs written clearly enough for junior team members to produce first drafts without clarification.
  • The content quality gate: nothing is published without passing through this role first.
  • AI tool usage as a productivity layer, not a substitute for thinking.

What You Will Not Own

  • SEO keyword selection (handled by the SEO Specialist).
  • Social media scheduling and publishing (handled by a separate team member).
  • Visual design of content assets (handled by the Visual Designer).
  • Distribution strategy (decided by the Marketing & Growth Lead).
  • ICP definition (you write for the ICP, but do not define it).

Requirements

  • Minimum 3 to 5 years writing B2B content (strong candidates have 5–6 years).
  • Content that ranked on Google, not just published.
  • Experience writing in voices other than your own (executives, founders, senior professionals).
  • Working-level SEO understanding (search intent, writing to intent).
  • Experience with AI writing tools and their limitations.
  • Content that contributed to measurable outcomes (traffic, leads, engagement).
  • Background in technology, SaaS, or professional services preferred.

Writing Ability

  • Writes with a clear point of view, not neutral summaries.
  • Explains complex technical concepts in plain language without losing credibility.
  • Writes concisely with no filler or unnecessary qualification.
  • Adapts to different voices authentically.

Mindset

  • Treats content as a commercial tool, not a creative exercise.
  • Comfortable with feedback and does not treat it as personal criticism.
  • Genuinely curious about AI, technology, and business operations.
  • Fast-paced: the team cannot wait three days for a first draft.

What We Are Not Looking For

  • Portfolios of generic "Top 10 Tips" articles or trend summaries with no original thinking.
  • Writers who cannot explain how their content performed or its contribution.
  • Writers without experience targeting technical or senior business audiences.
  • Writers who only produce self-directed content and lack consistency with briefs.
  • Candidates who cannot write convincingly in a voice other than their own.
  • Candidates who treat AI tools as the primary author with minimal editing.

Benefits

  • A growth-driven environment with opportunities to lead, innovate, and upskill continuously.

Contact: If this opportunity aligns with your career goals, kindly share your updated resume at careers@2basetechnologies.com.

Organic Growth & SEO Specialist

2Base Technologies Pvt Ltd
Infopark

Strategic SEO role building a scalable organic search engine for US/UK markets. Owns technical architecture, keyword targeting, and high-intent page scaling.

3-5 YearsSEO StrategyTechnical SEOProgrammatic SEO
Apply by: 10 Apr 2026

Organic Growth & SEO Specialist

2Base Technologies is building its marketing function from a clear brief, and this role owns the organic search engine that sits at the center of it. We are a technology services company with over 15 years of delivery experience, working with mid-market and enterprise clients across the United States and the United Kingdom. Our work spans AI implementation, custom software development, legacy system modernization, and operational transformation.

What This Role Exists to Do

This role does not optimize content after it is written. It determines what gets written, why, and how it is structured so that the right people find it at the right moment in their decision process. The organic search function at 2Base is being built to generate qualified inbound pipeline from two specific markets, the US and UK, at scale. That means a large volume of high-intent pages, a technical foundation that performs, and a programmatic architecture that compounds over time. The person who fills this role designs that system and owns its results.

What You Will Own

  • The organic traffic strategy for the US and UK markets, including keyword targeting and the full architecture of how search drives inbound pipeline
  • Keyword research and search intent mapping across all service lines and target audiences
  • Page architecture of the website, including what pages exist, what they target, how they are structured, and how they connect through internal linking
  • On-page SEO across all published pages
  • Technical SEO oversight, working directly with the development team on crawlability, indexing, site speed, Core Web Vitals, and structured data
  • Google Search Console as a working instrument, including weekly review, issue resolution, and opportunity identification
  • The programmatic SEO build, including designing the framework and templates that allow the site to scale to 80 to 120+ high-intent pages
  • SEO briefs written clearly enough that the Content Specialist can execute without guessing
  • Link building target approval. The outreach team identifies candidates, and you approve or reject based on defined quality standards
  • SEO performance reporting, including organic traffic, keyword movement, pages published, and Search Console health

What You Will Not Own

  • Writing content: you brief the Content Specialist, you do not write the pages
  • Link building outreach: a dedicated team member executes this, you set the standard
  • Paid search: that is a separate role
  • Social media distribution: separate channel, separate owner
  • Content calendar scheduling: the Marketing & Growth Lead sets distribution priorities

Requirements

  • Minimum 3 to 5 years in an SEO or organic growth role, with strong candidates typically at the 4 to 6-year mark
  • Experience ranking high-intent commercial pages, not just informational content
  • Experience managing technical SEO independently
  • Experience building or contributing to a programmatic SEO architecture
  • Strong working knowledge of Google Search Console as an active tool
  • Experience working across US and/or UK markets
  • Working knowledge of AEO, GEO, and AIO, including structuring content for AI-powered search surfaces
  • Ability to write SEO briefs that a content writer can execute without clarification

Mindset

  • Thinks in systems, not tasks
  • Comfortable with ambiguity in early-stage environments
  • Analytically honest, able to diagnose issues and adjust direction
  • Collaborative but not passive, working closely with content and development teams

What We Are Not Looking For

  • SEO practitioners whose entire experience is informational content
  • Candidates who treat Search Console as a monthly reporting task
  • Candidates who cannot explain high-intent vs. informational keyword targeting
  • Candidates whose SEO process depends entirely on tools
  • Candidates with no exposure to US/UK search behavior

Benefits

  • A growth-driven environment with opportunities to lead, innovate, and upskill continuously.

Contact: If this opportunity aligns with your career goals, kindly share your updated resume at careers@2basetechnologies.com.

What We Are Not Looking For

Sr. Visual Designer

2Base Technologies Pvt Ltd
Infopark

Senior Visual Designer to build brand system and create B2B marketing assets with precision and consistency for senior audiences.

3-5 YearsFigmaAdobe Creative SuiteBrand System Design
Apply by: 10 Apr 2026

Senior Visual Designer at 2Base Technologies

2Base Technologies is building its marketing function from scratch, and this role makes it look like a company worth taking seriously. We are a technology services company with over 15 years of delivery experience, working with mid-market and enterprise clients across the United States and the United Kingdom. Our work spans AI implementation, custom software development, legacy system modernisation, and operational transformation.

What This Role Exists to Do

Before a CTO reads a word of our content, they see the design. Before they trust the argument, they have already made a judgment about whether this company looks credible. This role owns that first impression, and then owns every asset that follows.

The visual function at 2Base is being built from the ground up. There is no brand system to inherit, no template library to use, and no consistent visual identity to maintain. What exists is a clear strategic direction, a defined audience of senior technology and operations leaders, and a marketing team building the content engine around it. Your job is to give that engine a visual identity it deserves.

The first 30 days of this role have one priority: build the brand system. Everything else, including LinkedIn carousels, ad creatives, landing pages, and presentation templates, is built from that foundation. A designer who wants to jump straight into production before the system exists is not the right fit.

This is not a creative agency role. The audience is sceptical, senior, and technically literate. Design that looks clever but reads as unclear, or feels consumer-facing rather than professional, will not work with this ICP. Restraint, precision, and consistency matter more than visual novelty.

What You Will Own

  • The 2Base visual brand system, including colour palette, typography, spacing, layout rules, and the documentation that makes it usable by the whole team
  • All marketing and content visual assets, including LinkedIn carousels, single-image posts, social graphics, infographics, and diagrams
  • Paid advertising creatives, including Google Display and LinkedIn Ads, designed to be tested and iterated
  • Landing page visual design, including layout, components, and conversion-focused structure, handed to the development team for build
  • Email visual templates, presentation templates, and sales deck templates
  • A template library that enables other team members to produce on-brand assets independently
  • Design consistency auditing, including periodic review of all published assets to ensure alignment with the brand system
  • Secondary responsibility: light video editing and motion for social reels, YouTube, and website use, supporting other team members

What You Will Not Own

  • What an asset communicates. The Content and Thought Leadership Specialist owns the message, argument, and information hierarchy. You may suggest improvements in structure, but content decisions remain with them
  • Copywriting. The Content Specialist writes the words; you structure them visually
  • Website development. You design the pages; the development team builds them
  • Content strategy. You execute what is briefed, not decide what gets created
  • Brand positioning. The Marketing Operating System defines how 2Base communicates; you interpret it visually

Requirements

  • Experience: Minimum 3 to 5 years in a B2B design role, preferably in technology, SaaS, or professional services
  • Experience building a brand system or significantly evolving one, not just producing isolated assets
  • Experience designing for LinkedIn, including carousel formats, document posts, and single-image feed content
  • Experience creating paid ad creatives that have been executed, tested, and iterated
  • Experience designing landing pages with an understanding of conversion principles
  • Comfort with basic video editing for social and web content, including reels, short-form YouTube, and simple website assets
  • Proficiency in Figma, which is non-negotiable, and Adobe Creative Suite including Photoshop, Illustrator, Premiere Pro, and After Effects
  • Design thinking
  • Portfolio demonstrates restraint through clean, structured, and purposeful design
  • Ability to explain the reasoning behind key design decisions
  • Designs with a specific audience in mind, not for general appeal
  • Strong understanding and consistent application of typography as a functional tool
  • Ability to produce work that appears credible to a senior B2B audience at first glance

Mindset

  • Able to work effectively from structured briefs
  • Works at speed without compromising quality
  • Treats design as a communication tool rather than purely creative expression
  • Open to feedback and able to give it constructively

What We Are Not Looking For

  • Portfolios dominated by consumer brands, lifestyle work, event design, or campaigns with no B2B relevance
  • Designers who can describe visuals but cannot justify their decisions
  • Candidates without experience building a brand system
  • Designers who overcomplicate visuals with excessive fonts, colours, styles, or effects
  • Candidates who require complete creative freedom and struggle with structured briefs

Benefits

  • A growth-driven environment with opportunities to lead, innovate, and upskill continuously.

If this opportunity aligns with your career goals, kindly share your updated resume with us at careers@2basetechnologies.com.

QA Engineer

We are seeking a detail-oriented Associate QA Engineer with 1–3 years of hands-on experience in software testing to join our QA team. In this role, you will ensure the quality and reliability of web and mobile applications by participating in test planning, test case creation, test execution, and defect tracking.

Key Responsibilities:

  • Review BRD, SRS, user stories, and functional specifications to understand system requirements.
  • Translate requirements into structured test scenarios and documented test cases for comprehensive coverage.
  • Perform functional, regression, and exploratory testing across web and mobile platforms.
  • Identify edge cases, alternate flows, and boundary conditions to validate system behavior.
  • Log, document, and track defects with clear reproduction steps and severity classification.
  • Validate bug fixes and perform regression testing during releases.
  • Maintain test documentation, execution reports, and QA artifacts for traceability.
  • Support test summaries, progress updates, and QA reports during development cycles.
  • Collaborate with business analysts, developers, and senior QA engineers to resolve issues.
  • Participate in Agile/Scrum ceremonies (sprint planning, stand-ups, reviews).
  • Perform basic API validation and data verification for integration-level testing.
  • Own assigned modules/features to ensure testing completeness and release readiness.
  • Contribute to improving test coverage, testing approaches, and QA processes.
  • Validate AI-powered/data-driven features for output accuracy and system behavior.
  • Learn automation fundamentals and emerging QA tools like AI testing practices.

Required Skills & Mindset:

  • Strong attention to detail and structured thinking.
  • Willingness to understand business logic before testing.
  • Ability to identify edge cases and risks beyond happy paths.
  • Analytical mindset to question unexpected system behavior.
  • Clear communication and collaboration skills.
  • Solid documentation for defect reporting and test case writing.
  • Experience with manual testing, test documentation, and defect reporting.
  • Basic exposure to automation and modern QA tools.
  • Familiarity with test case design techniques.
  • Experience with bug tracking and test management tools.
  • Basic API testing knowledge (Postman, REST Assured).
  • Understanding of Agile/Scrum methodologies and QA’s role in sprints.
  • Familiarity with AI-assisted testing.

Good to Have:

  • Awareness of performance and security testing.
  • Interest in learning automation frameworks (Selenium, Playwright, Cypress).
  • Basic scripting in Python, JavaScript, or Java.
  • Exposure to AI-enabled systems (chatbots, recommendation engines).
  • Awareness of continuous testing in modern pipelines.
  • Experience with mobile testing frameworks (Appium).
  • Risk-based testing prioritization.
  • Commitment to continuous learning and QA tool updates.
  • ISTQB certification or equivalent.

Business Analyst

The Business Analyst plays a key role in ensuring requirements are clearly understood, accurately documented, and traceable throughout the software development lifecycle. This role focuses on translating business and functional inputs into structured, standardized documentation that supports effective development, testing, and delivery. Working closely with business analysts, design teams, and technical stakeholders, the role ensures consistency, clarity, and alignment across all requirement artifacts.

Key Responsibilities

  • Create Software Requirement Specifications (SRS) based on inputs from Core Business Analysts, stakeholder discussions, and requirement walkthroughs
  • Prepare Business Requirement Documents (BRD) using approved templates while ensuring business intent and system behavior are clearly documented
  • Participate in requirement discussions to understand business objectives, functional flows, dependencies, and assumptions before documentation
  • Analyze requirements to identify gaps, ambiguities, and inconsistencies, and work with Core BAs to resolve them
  • Document functional flows, business rules, and acceptance criteria where applicable to support development and QA teams
  • Document wireframes, UI flows, validations, and UI specifications in collaboration with design and product teams
  • Maintain change logs, version history, and document updates throughout the project lifecycle
  • Create and manage traceability matrices linking business, functional, and technical requirements
  • Maintain cross-references across BRD, SRS, UI, API, and related documentation
  • Ensure documentation consistency, completeness, and alignment with approved scope and delivery timelines
  • Ensure accurate and timely PMS updates with structured documentation details
  • Support development, QA, UAT, and audit processes through clear, traceable, and up-to-date documentation
  • Assist in requirement reviews, walkthroughs, and validation sessions with internal and client stakeholders

Required Skills and Experience

  • 1 to 3 years of experience in Business Analysis or related roles
  • Strong experience in BRD and SRS creation
  • Hands-on experience with documentation templates, standards, and version control
  • Ability to document UI wireframes and functional flows clearly
  • Working knowledge of APIs and system integrations for documentation purposes
  • Experience with project management systems and documentation tools
  • Strong attention to detail and ability to manage multiple documents in parallel
  • Excellent written communication and stakeholder coordination skills

Minimum Qualifications

  • Bachelor’s degree in Engineering, Computer Science, Information Systems, or a related field
  • 1 to 3 years of experience as a Business Analyst or Product Analyst

Benefits

  • A growth-driven environment with opportunities to lead, innovate, and upskill continuously.

Software Engineer - Web

Sr. Business Analyst

It is not a support role. This is a core Business Analyst position responsible for functional modelling, system reasoning, requirement clarity, and building the foundation for correct development.

Key Responsibilities

  • Lead requirement workshops, client calls, and discovery discussions to understand business needs clearly.
  • Ask deeper questions, challenge assumptions, and validate the true business intent behind every requirement.
  • Convert ambiguous client inputs into structured, logical, and actionable functional understanding.
  • Break large features into modules, workflows, components, and clear dependencies.
  • Build strong system-level understanding involving APIs, integrations, data flow, and backend considerations.
  • Translate business processes into functional logic that development teams can execute.
  • Decompose requirements into use-case flows, system behaviours, edge cases, alternate paths, validation rules, and dependencies.
  • Prepare high-quality documentation, including BRD, FRD, SRS, workflows, state diagrams, data-flow diagrams, API requirement specs, and acceptance criteria.
  • Ensure all documentation is clear, logical, structured, testable, and ready for developers and QA to use.
  • Collaborate closely with developers, architects, QA, and product owners to validate feasibility and align understanding.
  • Ensure QA teams can derive test cases effectively from your functional logic and acceptance criteria.
  • Communicate confidently with clients, handle requirement discussions smoothly, and clarify misunderstandings immediately.
  • Push back politely on unclear or changing requirements and ensure final decisions are documented properly.
  • Maintain requirement traceability throughout the lifecycle and ensure zero ambiguity during handover to development.
  • Own the entire requirement lifecycle from discovery to development readiness with high accountability.
  • Drive clarity across teams by ensuring every requirement is complete, validated, and logically consistent.

Required Skills & Experience

  • Minimum 4+ years of core Business Analyst experience with strong analytical and system-level thinking.
  • Ability to break down complex requirements into clear components, workflows, and functional logic.
  • Excellent verbal and written communication with confidence in client interactions and clarifications.
  • Proven experience in preparing SRS, BRD, FRD, workflows, and acceptance criteria with high clarity.
  • Ability to challenge assumptions politely, ask the right questions, and ensure zero ambiguity.
  • Strong collaboration experience with development, QA, architects, and cross-functional teams.
  • Understanding of API behaviours, integrations, data flows, and multi-module system interactions.
  • Ability to run requirement discussions, workshops, and independently lead discovery sessions.
  • Exposure to SaaS, scalable products, automation, or AI-supported systems is an added advantage.
  • Demonstrated ownership of requirements end-to-end, ensuring developer-ready and testable outputs.
  • Not suitable for UI-only thinkers, passive communicators, template-based writers, or those relying on AI for answers.
  • Success is defined by clear, testable requirements, zero rework, strong cross-team alignment, and confident communication.
  • Candidates must align with 2Base’s structured thinking, clarity-driven culture, and transformation of the BA function.

Minimum Qualifications

  • Bachelor’s degree in Computer Science, Engineering, Business, or related field
  • 4 to 8 years of experience as a Business Analyst or Product Analyst
  • Experience in SaaS or scalable product environments
  • Exposure to AI/Automation, integrations, or multi-module systems

Job Description: Security Engineering Leader (US)

Company: Reflections Info Systems (P) Ltd Location: Thiruvananthapuram, Kerala, India Contact Email: Careers@reflectionsinfos.com Closing Date: 17, Apr 2026 Job Published: 10, Apr 2026

Overview

We are seeking a 12+ years experienced Security Engineering Leader to drive enterprise security initiatives across DLP, PAM, password management, penetration testing, and access governance.

Key Responsibilities

Security Project Delivery

  • Own the full lifecycle of enterprise security projects (charter, plan, execute, measure, close).
  • Lead simultaneous workstreams in DLP, PAM, password management, pentesting, and access reviews.
  • Establish governance cadences, status reporting, RAID logs, and steering-committee presentations.
  • Drive outcomes through matrixed teams, ensuring accountability across stakeholders.

Data Loss Prevention (DLP)

  • Architect and deploy DLP policies across endpoints, email, cloud (M365/Purview), and network egress.
  • Define data classification schemas with Legal/Compliance/business leaders.
  • Tune DLP rules to reduce false positives while protecting PII, client data, and proprietary info.
  • Establish incident response workflows and executive reporting metrics.

Privileged Access Management (PAM)

  • Lead enterprise PAM platform rollout (e.g., CyberArk, BeyondTrust) and governance.
  • Define vaulting, session-recording, and just-in-time access policies for hybrid infrastructure.
  • Drive adoption with Infrastructure/Cloud/application teams.
  • Close coverage gaps via structured roadmap initiatives.

Password Management

  • Design enterprise password strategies for workforce and privileged accounts (e.g., 1Password, Bitwarden).
  • Integrate tools with SSO, MFA, and identity governance platforms.
  • Embed credential security into onboarding/offboarding workflows.

Penetration Testing & Vulnerability Management

  • Manage pentesting programs (vendor selection, scheduling, remediation tracking).
  • Coordinate red-team/purple-team exercises and validate remediation closure.
  • Produce executive-grade summaries for CISO, CTO, and board audiences.

Access Reviews & Identity Governance

  • Operationalize continuous access reviews for AD, Entra ID, and SaaS apps.
  • Automate workflows with IGA platforms (e.g., SailPoint, Saviynt).
  • Enforce RBAC/least-privilege principles with HR/Compliance/application owners.
  • Support audits (SOX, PCAOB) with evidence packages.

Stakeholder Engagement

  • Serve as security liaison to business-unit leaders, framing initiatives as business enablers.
  • Present program status and risk posture to C-suite and board stakeholders.
  • Collaborate with Legal, Compliance, HR, and Finance to align with regulatory obligations.
